  <script data-rh="true">
   window.__KBB_LOGGER__={"appName":"homepage","branchid":"master","watchAds":true,"watchResources":true,"watchTti":true,"watchWebVitals":true,"watchedResources":["moat"]};

  <script data-rh="true" id="loadBundlesScript" type="text/javascript">
   var bundlesWorker = (function () {
        function logToNR(message) {
          if (typeof window === 'undefined' || typeof window.NREUM === 'undefined' || typeof window.NREUM.noticeError !== 'function') {
            console.log(message);
          }
          else {
            window.NREUM.noticeError(message);
          }
        }
        function initWorker() {
          if (!useWorker()) {
            return;
          }
          let workerCommands = ['loadJS', 'stats'];
          let workerPath = '/shared-resources/workers/bundle.worker.1.min.js';
          this.worker = new Worker(workerPath);
          this.worker.addEventListener('error', function (e) {
            logToNR('Error in bundle worker: Line ' + e.lineno + ' in ' +  e.filename + ': ' + e.message);
          });
          this.worker.addEventListener('message', function (e) {
            if (e && e.data && !!e.data.cmd && workerCommands.indexOf(e.data.cmd >= 0)) {
              try {
                let msgData = e.data;
                switch (msgData.cmd) {
                  case 'loadJS':
                    head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
                    script = document.createElement('script');
                    script[script.innerText ? 'innerText' : 'textContent'] = msgData.data;
                    head.appendChild(script);
                    break;
                  case 'stats':
                    console.info('Worker Stats: ', JSON.stringify(msgData.data));
                    break;
                  default:
                    return;
                }
              }
              catch (err) {
                console.log(err);
              }
            }
          }, false);
        }
        function getStats() {
          if (typeof this.worker !== 'undefined') {
            this.worker.postMessage({
              cmd: 'stats'
            });
          }
        }
        function useWorker() {
          if (!!window.Worker && !(window.location.href.lastIndexOf('noworker') >= 0)) {
            return true;
          }
          return false;
        }
        function loadBundles(jsBundles, keepOrder) {
          if (useWorker()) {
            if (typeof this.worker === 'undefined') {
              initWorker();
            }
            this.worker.postMessage({
              cmd: 'loadJS',
              bundles: jsBundles,
              keepOrder: keepOrder
            });
          }
          else {
            jsBundles.forEach(function (bundle) {
              head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
              script = document.createElement('script');
              script.src = bundle;
              script.defer = true;
              head.appendChild(script);
            });
          }
        }
        return {
          initWorker: initWorker,
          getStats: getStats,
          loadBundles: loadBundles
        }
      })();
      bundlesWorker.initWorker();
  </script>
